\bentry
\wordRemoveSpace{V-v}{V v}
\pron{viV} 
\gl{\nA}
\expl{(\bava\ \eng{Vs} yA \eng{V's}).}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} iMgilxSf vaNaRmAleya ipapxtetxraDaneya akaSxra. 
\num{2} mara \mo vugaLa paTiTxgaLa \eng{V} AkArada joVDaNe. 
\num{3} \eng{V} AkArada vasutx. 
\num{4} roVmanf saMKAyx saMkeVtadalilx aidu. 
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\pron{?}
\gl{\saMkiSx}

\bmng
 \eng{(V.} saha) \eng{volt(s).} 
\emng

\bentry
\word{vac}
\pron{vAYxkf} 
\gl{\nA}
\expl{}
\bmng
 (\birx)(\AmA) (\kanmu\ vishavxvidAyxnilayagaLa) \eng{vacation} (\saMkiSx). 
\emng
\eentry

\bentry
\word{vacancy} 
\pron{veVkanisx} 
\gl{\nA}
\expl{(\bava\ \eng{vacancies}).}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} baridAgiruvike; KAliyAgiruvike. 
\num{2} shUnayxmanasakxte; jaDamanasakxte; manasisxna niSikxrXya sithxti. 
\num{3} KAli hudedx yA sAthxna: \eng{he has no vacancy on his staff} Atana sibabxMdi vagaRdalilx yAva KAli sAthxnavU ilalx. \eng{no vacancies at present in this office} sadayxdalilx I kaceVriyalilx yAva hudedxgaLU KAli ilalx. 
\num{4} (hoVTelu \mo vugaLalilx) laBayxviruva KAli koVNe, rUmu. 
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\bentry
\word{vacant} 
\pron{veVkaMTf} 
\gl{\gu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} baridAgiruva; KAli(yAgiruva); BatiRyAgilalxda: \eng{the house is still vacant} A mane inUnx KAli ide. 
\num{2} biDuvAgiruva; yAva kelasavU ilalxde virAmavAgiruva: \eng{this will amuse your vacant hours} ninanx biDuvAda, virAmada, hotitxnalilx idu ninage vinoVdavanunx koDutatxde. 
\num{3} terapAgiruva; KAli iruva: \eng{he applied for a vacant post} avanu terapAgidadx, KAli idadx, oMdu hudedxgAgi ajiR hAkikoMDa. 
\num{4} shUnayxmanasakxnAda; vicAra, BAva -- shUnayx Ada; niSikxrXya, jaDa -- manasakxnAda: \eng{his mind seems completely vacant} avanu saMpUNaRvAgi shUnayxmanasakxnaMtidAdxne. \eng{a vacant stare} shUnayxdaqSiTx; gamanakekx tegedukoLaLxde neTaTx daqSiTxyiMda elolxV noVDutitxruvudu. 
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\bentry

\pron{vAYxkuyxamf} 
\gl{\nA}

\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} shUnayxparxdeVsha; yAvudeV vasutxvilalxda parxdeVsha. 
\num{2} nivARta -- pAterx, parxdeVsha; vAyuvanunx hecucxkaDime saMpUNaRvAgi tegaduhAkibiTiTxruva pAterx yA parxdeVsha: \eng{Torricellian vacuum} TAriceliyanf nivARtaparxdeVsha. 
\num{3} vAyuviraLate; vAyuvina otatxDa yA saMmadaR sAmAnayxvAgi irabeVkAda parxmANakikxMta kaDimeyAgiruvudu. 
\num{4} aBAva; rAhitayx; yAvudeV sathxLa, saninxveVsha, \mo vugaLalilx irabeVkAda vayxkitx, vasutx, caTuvaTike, \mo vu ilalxdiruvudu. 
\num{5} (\AmA) (\bava\ \eng{vacuums}) = \hyperlink{vacuum-cleaner}{vacuum-cleaner}.

\bentry 
\word[vapour(1)]{vapour} 
\pron{veVparf} 
\gl{\nA}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} habe; dhUma; (vAyumaMDaladalilx kaMDubaruva) maMju (rUpada teVva) yA hoge. 
\num{2} (\Bwvi) Avi; bASapx; sAmAnayxvAgi darxvasithxtiyalilxruva, viraLavAgi (kelavu padAthaRgaLa \vi) Ganasithxtiyalilxruva padAthaRda anilarUpa. 
\num{3} (\veYshA) habe; auSadhiyAgi usirADuvudakekx baLasuva yAvudeV padAthaR. 
\num{4} poLuLxkalapxne; huruLilalxda, nijavalalxda -- vasutx yA viSaya; \eng{it's all mere vapoury} adelalx bariya poLuLxkalapxne. 
\numi{5} (\bava dalilx) (\pArxparx) 
\banum
\alnum{a} (manasisxna) maMku; manoVmAlinayx; viSaNaNxte; gAlxni; vAyxkulate. 
\alnum{b} (unAmxda \mo\ yAvudeV bageya) manoVvikAra. 
\eanum

\bentry
\word[variable(1)]{variable} 
\pron{veVriabflf} 
\gl{\gu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} (beVkAda riVti) badalAyisabahudAda; mApaRDisabahudAda; hoMdisikoLaLxbahudAda; vayxtAyxsasAdhayx: \eng{a rod of variable length} udadxvanunx mApaRDisikoLaLx bahudAda salAki. \eng{the pressure is variable} otatxDavu badalAyisuvaMthadu. 
\num{2} (kAru \mo vugaLa giyarina \vi) veVgavanunx badalAyisabahudAda. 
\num{3} badalAyisuva parxvaqtitxyuLaLx; asithxra; caMcala. \eng{variable mood} asithxra manoVvaqtitx. \eng{variable fortune} caMcalavAda adaqSaTx, BAgayx. 
\num{4} (gALiya \vi) dikukx badalAyisutatxleV iruva. 
\num{5} (\Kavi) (tAreya \vi) caMcala; kAMtiyu AvataRniVyavAgi badalAguva. 
\num{6} (\ga) cara; (\sA\ biVjagaNitiVya saMkeVtada \vi) vividha saMKAyxmwlayxviruva; anidiRSaTx mUlayxda. 
\numi{7} 
\banum
\alnum{a} (\jiVvi\ matutx \savi) (jiVvijAtiya \vi) jAtiya vishiSaTxte ilalxdiruva jiVvigaLanonxLagoMDa. 
\alnum{b} (\jiVvi) (jiVviya yA adara aMgada \vi) vayxtayxyasAdhayx; racane matutx kirxye badalAguva sAdhayxteyuLaLx.

\bentry
\word{variance} 
\pron{veVrianfsx} 
\gl{\nA}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} aBipArxyaBeVda; vivAda; mataBeVda; BinAnxBipArxya: \eng{I have had a slight variance with him} avanigU nanagU savxlapx mataBeVda uMTAgide. \eng{on that point we are at variance (among ourselves)} A viSayavanunx kuritu namamxnamamxlilx BinAnxBipArxyavide. 
\num{2} vAyxjayx; virasa; veYmanasayx: \eng{he is at variance with the authorities} avanigU adhikArigaLigU virasavide, veYmanasayxvide. 
\num{3} vayxtAyxsa; BeVda; tAratamayx: \eng{this theory is at variance with all that is known on the subject} A shAsatxrXda viSayadalilx iduvaregU tiLidiruva sakalakUkx I sidAdhxMtakUkx vayxtAyxsavide. 
\num{4} (\nAyxshA) heVLike heVLikegU yA patarxpatarxkUkx naDuve kaMDubaruva -- vayxtAyxsa, BeVda, tAratamayx, asAmaMjasayx. 
\num{5} (\saMshA) vipalalxTa; parxmANaka vicalana yA dikucxyXtiya \eng{(standard deviation)} vagaR. 
\num{6} (\ame) mAmUlu niyamagaLanunx biTuTx kAyaRniNaRya yA kAyaR mADalu koDalAda anumati; (niyamadiMdAce hoVguva) viveVcanAdhikAra.

\bentry
\word{variation} 
\pron{veVriESanf} 
\gl{\nA}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} badalAvaNe; mApARDu; parivataRne: \eng{prices are subject to variation} belegaLu badalAvaNege oLapaTiTxve; belegaLu badalAvaNegoLuLxva saMBavavide. 
\num{2} (hiMdina yA sahaja sithxtiyiMda, kirxyeyalilx yA motatxdalilx, Aguva) vayxtAyxsa yA A vayxtAyxsada parxmANa: \eng{repeated variations of temperature} (havAmAna \mo vugaLalilx) matetxmatetx Aguva tApa(parxmANa)da badalAvaNegaLu, tApAMtaragaLu. \eng{it is subject to variation of several degrees} adara tApadalilx halavu DigirxgaLaSuTx vayxtAyxsa Aguva saMBavavide. 
\num{3} (\Kavi) cuyxti; KAgoVLika kAyavu tananx sarAsari kakeSx yA calaneyanunx biTuTxhoVguvudu. 
\num{4} (\ga) vayxtayxyana; Palana oMdaralilxna sithxragaLu \mo vugaLalAlxguva alapx badalAvaNeya PalavAgi PalanadalAlxguva badalAvaNe. 
\num{5} (mAdarigiMta, namUnegiMta, parxmANakikxMta, jAti yA vagaRkikxMta) BinanxvAda vasutx, viSaya. 
\num{6} (\saM) rAgaBeVda yA viSayaBeVda; kaqtiyanunx hADuvalilx yA vAdana mADuvalilx gAyakanu yA vAdanakAranu mADuva rAgada yA viSayada BeVda yA avugaLa visatxraNa. 
\num{7} (bAYxle naqtayx) Eka nataRka yA nataRki naqtayx.

\bentry
\word{variety} 
\pron{vareYaTi} 
\gl{\nA}
\expl{(\bava\ \eng{varieties}). }
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} bagebage(yAgiruvudu); vividhate; veYvidhayx: \eng{variety} \eng{of the scenery} A daqshAyxvaLiya veYvidhayx. \eng{Bangalore has the charm of variety} beMgaLUru nagarakekx veYvidhayxda moVhakate ide. 
\num{2} bahumuKate: \eng{the variety of his conversation} avana saMBASaNeyalilx kaMDubaruva bahumuKate. 
\num{3} bagebageya, vividha, nAnA bageya -- vasutxgaLu yA viSayagaLu yA avugaLa samudAya: \eng{a variety of books} bagebageya pusatxkagaLu. \eng{a variety of reasons} nAnA bageya kAraNagaLu. 
\hypertarget{variety(4)}{} 
\num{4} vividha vinoVdAvaLi; naqtayx, gAyana, hAsAyxBinaya, \mo vugaLa parxdashaRna kAyaRkarxma. 
\num{5} (\jiVvi) upajAti; sAmAnayx lakaSxNagaLalilx parxdhAna jAtivoMdariMda BinanxvAda oMdu upajAti yA adaralolxMdu pArxNi. 
\numi{6} (\jiVvi) 
\banum
\alnum{a} upajAti; oMdeV jAtige seVridudAgi, jAtiyoLage punarutapxtitx sAdhayxviruva, Adare AnuvaMshika lakaSxNagaLu savxlapxmaTiTxge BinanxvAgiruva vayxkitx yA guMpu. 
\alnum{b} = \hyperref{kandict_c.pdf}{C}{cultivar}{cultivar}. 
\eanum
\numie
\enum
\emng

\bentry
\word{vary} 
\pron{veVri} 
\gl{\kirx} 
\bmng
(vataRmAna \parxpu\ \Eva\ \eng{varies}; \BU\ matutx  \BUkaq\ \eng{varied}).
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\sakirx}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} badalAyisu; mApaRDisu; vayxtAyxsagoLisu: \eng{we can vary the pressure at will} otatxDavanunx, saMmadaRvanunx, nAvu beVkAdaMte mApaRDisabahudu. \eng{he seldom varies the routine} dinacariyanunx avanu badalAyisuvudu tiVra viraLa, bahushaH badalAyisuvudilalx. \eng{the doctor varies the treatment according to circumstances} veYdayxnu cikitAsxvidhAnavanunx saMdaBoRVcitavAgi vayxtAyxsa mADutAtxne. 
\num{2} veYvidhayxgoLisu: \eng{his style is not sufficiently varied} avana sheYliyalilx sAkaSuTx veYvidhayxvilalx. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\akirx}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} (guNa, rUpa, pariNAma, \mo vugaLalilx) badalAyisu; badalAvaNeyAgu; vayxtAyxsavAgu: \eng{his mood varies from day to day} avana manasusx, manaHsithxti dinadiMda dinakekx badalAyisutitxrutatxde. \eng{the temperature varies from} \eng{$30^\circ$} \eng{to} \eng{$70^\circ$} tApamAnavu \eng{$30^\circ$} yiMda \eng{$70^\circ$} ge vayxtAyxsavAgutatxde. 
\num{2} beVreyAgiru; BinanxvAgiru: \eng{this varies from the type} idu tananx jAtiyiMda BinanxvAgide, beVre bageyadAgide. 
\num{3} beVrebeVreyAgiru; bagebageyAgiru; vividhavAgiru; Binanx BinanxvAgiru: \eng{opinions vary on this point} I viSayadalilx aBipArxyagaLu bagebageyAgive, BinanxBinanxvAgive. 
\num{4} anuguNavAgiru; anusAravAgi, anuguNavAgi badalAvaNe hoMdu: \eng{the demand varies with the season} beVDike kAlakekx anuguNavAgirutatxde, anuguNavAgi vayxtAyxsavAgutatxde. 
\num{5} (\ga) (anuloVmavAgi yA viloVmavAgi) badalAyisu; Binanx mwlayxgaLanunx paDe: \eng{attraction of bodies varies directly as their masses and inversely as the square of their distance} kAyagaLa parasapxra AkaSaRNe avugaLa parimANakekx anuloVmavAgi matutx dUrakekx viloVmavAgi vayxtAyxsavAgutatxde, badalAyisutatxde. 
\enum
\emng

\bentry
\word[verbal(1)]{verbal} 
\pron{vabaRlf} 
\gl{\gu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} padagaLa yA padagaLige saMbaMdhisida; shAbidxka yA shAbadx: \eng{verbal subtleties} shabadxsUkaSx mxtegaLu. \eng{verbal accuracy} pada niSakxqqSaTxte; niSakxqqSaTx padaparxyoVga. 
\num{2} shAbadx; shAbidxka; padagaLanunxLaLx yA padarUpada: \eng{verbal imagery} shAbadx, shAbidxka -- parxtime. 
\num{3} keVvala shabadxgaLige yA padagaLige saMbaMdhisida: \eng{a purely verbal distinction between two concepts} eraDu kalapxnegaLa naDuvaNa keVvala shAbidxka vayxtAyxsa. 
\num{4} vAcika; vAgUrxpada; bAyimAtina; mwKika: barahada mUlaka Agirade mAtina mUlaka tiLisida: \eng{verbal contract} bAyimAtina yA muKataH mADikoMDa -- karAru, opapxMda. \eng{verbal evidence} bAyimAtina, vAcA heVLida, mwKika -- sAkaSxyX. 
\num{5} (anuvAdada, tajuRmeya \vi) akaSxraniSaThx; padaniSaThx; akaSxrashaH, padashaH -- mADida. 
\num{6} (\vAyx) kirxyA padada yA rUpada: \eng{verbal inflexions} kirxyApadada kAla \eng{(tense)}, parxyoVga \eng{(voice)}, BAva \eng{(mood)}, vacana \eng{(number)} matutx puruSa \eng{(person)} eMba rUpAMtaragaLu yA rUpaBeVdagaLu. 
\num{7} vAcALiyAda. 
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\bentry
\word[verge(1)]{verge} 
\pron{vajfR} 
\gl{\nA}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum

\num{2} (\birx) (hUgiDada, rasetx, \mo vugaLa) hulilxna -- aMcu, arugu, diMDu, teMDe. 
\num{3} (\vAshi) caMdAyada, geVbalina heMcineVNina muMcAcu. 
\num{4} (biSapf, DiVnf, \mo vara muMde hiDidukoMDu hoVguva, avara padaviya lAMCanavAda) daMDa; doNeNx; kaTiTxge. 
\num{5} (\ca) (lADfR heY siTxVvaDfR eMba birxTaninxna rAjana yA rANiya kiriVTABiSeVkadalilx adhayxkaSxnAgi vatiRsuva adhikAriya) adhikAra vAyxpitxge oLapaTaTx parxdeVsha.

\emng

\bentry
\word{verify} 
\pron{veripheY} 
\gl{\sakirx}
\expl{(vataRmAna \parxpu\ \Eva\ \eng{verifies}; \BU\ matutx}
\BUkaq\ \eng{verified}). \bmng
\bnum
\num{1} sari, tALe, tAkaRNe -- noVDu: \eng{always verify your references} ninanx ulelxVKagaLanunx tapapxde sarinoVDu, sariyAgideye eMbaudanunx Kacita mADiko. 
\num{2} parishiVlane, parxyoVga yA pariVkeSxgaLa mUlaka viSayavu satayx yA sari eMbaudanunx rujuvAtupaDisu: \eng{I must verify his statement} avana heVLike nijave eMbaudanunx nAnu pariVkiSxsi noVDabeVku. 
\num{3} (GaTane, kAyaR, \mo vugaLa \vi) niriVkaSxNege, vAgAdxna, \mo vakekx -- anuguNavAgiru; niriVkaSxNe, vAgAdxna, \mo vanunx nijapaDisu. 
\numi{4} (\nAyxshA) 
\banum
\alnum{a} dAveyalilx sUcisiruva vAdagaLige yA parxtivAdagaLige keYPiyatatxnunx yA dAKaleyanunx lagatitxsu. 
\alnum{b} heVLikeyanunx rujuvAtugaLiMda yA parxmANapatarxdiMda (satayxveMdu) samathiRsu, daqDhapaDisu. 
\eanum
\numie
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\bentry
\word[very(1)]{very} 
\pron{veri} 
\gl{\gu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} (\pArxparx) nijavAda; vAsatxvavAda; yathAthaRvAda; sAkASxtAtxda; sAcA: \eng{very God} nijavAda deVvaru. 
\num{2} parama; acacx; apapxTa; keVvala; shudAdhxMgavAda: \eng{the veriest simpleton knows that} shudadhx muTAThxLanU adanunx balalx. \eng{the very truth} parama satayx. \eng{must consent from very shame} keVvala nAcikegAdarU, apakiVtiRya BayakAkxdarU opapxleV beVku. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\eng{the, this, that, his, etc. very} ivaneV, ideV, avaneV, adeV, avana savxMta, itAyxdi athaRgaLalilx avadhAraNAthaRdalilx, otitxheVLuva \parx : \eng{this is the very spot where I found it} nanageadu doreta sathxLa, ideV. \eng{the very same} tadavxtAtxgiadeV. \eng{these were his very words} ivu avana savxMta mAtugaLu; ImAtugaLu avanaveV. \eng{speaking in this very room} I koThaDiyalelxVmAtanADutAtx. \eng{he did it this very day} avanu adanunx ideV dina,iMdeV mADida. \eng{the very fact of his presence is enough} avanuhAjarAgidadx eMba saMgatiyeV sAku. \eng{you are the very man I am looking for} nAnu huDukutitxruva vayxkitx niVneV. \eng{a needle is the very thing for our purpose} namamx udedxVshakekx beVkAda vasutxeMdare sUjiyeV. \eng{come here this very minute} I kaSxN(dalelxV)ililx bA. \eng{it grieves me to the very heart} adu nananxhaqdayAMtarALavanenxV vayxthegoLisutatxde. \eng{the very stones cry out} A kalulxgaLeV kUgi heVLutatxve. \eng{at the very edge of the cliff} A koVDugalilxna tutatx tudiyalilx. \eng{a very little will do} tiVra, keVvala savxlapx sAku. \eng{give me only a very little}nanage bahaLa savxlapx, oMdu cuTaku mAtarx koDu. \eentry

\bentry
\word[very(2)]{very} 
\pron{veri} 
\gl{\kirxvi}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\numi{1} (-tamarUpada \gu\ doDane). 
\banum
\alnum{a} atayxMta; kaTaTxkaDeya; atayxdhika; gariSaThx; paramAvadhi : \eng{drink it to the very last drop} adanunx kaTaTxkaDeya haniyavaregU kuDidubiDu. \eng{the very last thing I expected} (niSeVdhAthaRdalilx mAtarx) nAnu niriVkiSxsidadxralilx atayxMta kaDeyadu (eMdare adanunx nAnu niriVkiSxsiraleV ilalx). \eng{did the very best I could} nananx keYyalAlxda paramAvadhiyanunx mADide. \eng{did my very utmost} nananx atayxdhika parxyatanxvanUnx mADide. 
\alnum{b} \eng{own} padadoDane pUtiRyAgi; saMpUNARthaRdalilx: \eng{my very own room} nananxdeV koVNe. \eng{you may keep it for your very own} adanunx niVnu pUtiR ninanx savxMtakAkxgi iTuTxkoLaLxbahudu. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{2} (\gu gaLu, visheVSa kaqdaMtagaLu matutx \kirxvi gaLoDane) tuMba; bahaLa; bahu; balu; tiVra: \eng{that is very easy} adu bahaLa sulaBa. \eng{it is very annoying} adu tiVra kirikiriyanunxMTu mADuvaMthadu. \eng{it is very easily done} adanunx bahu sulaBavAgi mADabahudu. \eng{it is a very trying time} idu tiVra kaSaTxkaravAda kAla. \eng{it very often fails} adu bahuveVLe viPalavAgutatxde. \eng{we find very few instances} nidashaRnagaLu dorakuvudu tiVra viraLa. \eng{he gives very little trouble} avaniMdAguva sharxma atayxlapx. \eng{is very much better} bahumaTiTxge utatxmavAgidAdxne. \eng{I am very much annoyed} nanage tiVra kirikiriyuMTAgide. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent 
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}

\alnum{b} tiVra asaMBava. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{2} \eng{very good} (\engit{or} \eng{well)} (samamxti sUcisuvalilx) oLeLxyadu; Agali; sari; Ayitu. 
\enum
\emng

\bentry

\pron{veYsf} 
\gl{\nA}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\numi{1} 
\banum
\alnum{a} keTaTx -- guNa, savxBAva; aniVti; dubauRdidhx; avaguNa; durAcAra; duguRNa; dushishxVla: \eng{drunkenness is not among his vices} avana durAcAragaLalilx kuDitavu oMdalalx. 
\alnum{b} (veVshAyxvaqtitx, mAdakavasutxgaLu, \mo vanonxLagoMDa) pApa; pAtaka; hiVnakAyaR: \eng{vice is duly punished and virtue rewarded in the fifth act} aidaneya aMkadalilx pApakekx takakx shikeSxyAgi puNayxkekx salulxva parxtiPalavu doreyutatxde. 
\eanum
\numie
\numi{2} 
\banum
\alnum{a} niVtiBarxSaTxte; duSaTxtana; keVDu; duSakxqqtayx. 
\alnum{b} keTaTx cALi, caTa; duraBAyxsa: \eng{has the vice of gluttony} avanalilx hoTeTxbAkatanada duraBAyxsavide. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{3} (naDate yA naDavaLikeyalilx) doVSa; kaLaMka; nUyxnate. 
\num{4} (sAhitayxsheYli \mo vugaLa \vi) kuMdu; doVSa; nUyxnate. 
\num{5} (kudure \mo vugaLalilx) doVSa(gaLu) yA duraBAyxsa(gaLu). 
\num{6} (\ca) (niVtinATakada pAtarxgaLalilx) yAvudeV durAcAravanunx viDaMbana mADuva, pAtarx vahisuva koVDaMgi, vidUSaka pAtarx. 
\enum

\noindent 
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}

 \eng{redeeming vice} suguNAtireVkavanunx savxlapxmaTiTxge tagigxsuva duguRNa, doVSa: \eng{he has no redeeming vice} avana suguNAtireVkavanunx savxlapxmaTiTxge tagigxsuva yAvudeV duguRNavU avanalilxlalx.

\bentry
\word[view(1)]{view} 
\pron{vUyx} 
\gl{\nA}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} noVTa; viVkaSxNa; dashaRna; avaloVkana. 
\num{2} (\nAyxshA) (nAyxyadashiR maMDaliyu mokadadxmege saMbaMdhisida sathxLa, Asitx, \mo vanunx yA maqtadeVhavanunx) noVDuvudu; parishiVlane; pariVkaSxNa. 
\num{3} daqSiTx; noVTa; noVTada, kaNiNxna -- vAyxpitx: \eng{in full view of the crowd} guMpina kaNeNxdurinalelxV. \eng{the bird came into view} A pakiSx noVTada vAyxpitxge baMtu. \eng{the ship passed from our view} A haDagu namamx daqSiTxyiMda sariyitu, kaNamxreyAyitu. 
\num{4} noVTa; daqshayx; nidiRSaTx sAthxnadiMda noVDalapxTaTxdudx: \eng{the house has a view of the sea} A maneyiMda samudarxda noVTa sigutatxde, samudarx kANutatxde. \eng{a superb view} aduBxtavAda oMdu noVTa, Bavayxdaqshayx. 
\num{5} daqshayxcitarx; yAvudeV vasutx \mo vugaLa noVTavanunx oLagoMDiruva citarx. 
\num{6} daqSiTx; aBipArxya; BAvane; yAvudeV viSayavanunx -- noVDuva bage, kurita manoVBAva: \eng{he takes a different view} avanu beVre aBipArxyavanunx taLedidAdxne. \eng{his view is that we are aggressors} nAvu AkarxmaNakArareMbaudu avana BAvane. \eng{that is his view of her conduct} avaLa naDavaLikeya viSayadalilx avana daqSiTx adu. \eng{he holds extreme views (in politics etc. )} (rAjakiVya \mo vugaLalilx) avanu tiVvarxgAmi aBipArxyagaLanunx hoMdidAdxne. \eng{took a favourable view of the matter} viSayada bagegx anukUlakara aBipArxya taLeda. 
\num{7} udedxVsha; Ashaya; eNike: \eng{will this meet your views?} idu nimamx udedxVshagaLige sarihoMdutatxdeye? 
\num{8} viVkaSxNa; avaloVkana; pariVkaSxNa; samiVkaSxNa; cAkuSxSa yA mAnasika samiVkeSx; kaNiNxniMda yA mAnasikavAgi pariVkiSxsuvudu, taniKe mADuvudu. 
\num{9} viVkaSxNa; viVkaSxNAvakAsha: \eng{a view of the exhibition} parxdashaRnada viVkaSxNe, noVTa. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent 
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\numi{1} \eng{have in view} 
\banum
\alnum{a} (yAvudanenxV) guriyanAnxgi, udedxVshavanAnxgi hoMdiru. 
\alnum{b} (tiVmARnisuvAga, yAvudeV aMshavanunx) gamanadalilx, daqSiTxyalilx -- iTuTxkoMDiru. 
\eanum
\numie
\numi{2} \eng{in view of} 
\banum
\alnum{a} daqSiTxpathadalilx yA pathakekx; kaNiNxge biVLuva sAthxnadalilx: \eng{we came in view of the church} A cacuR kaNiNxge biVLuva sAthxnakekx baMdevu. \eng{he stood in view of the audience} avanu perxVkaSxkara daqSiTxpathadalilx niMta. 
\alnum{b} daqSiTxyiMda; noVDidare; noVDidalilx; gamanisidare; parigaNisidare; kAraNadiMda: \eng{in view of the recent developments, we do not think this step advisable} ititxVcina GaTanegaLanunx noVDidare, parigaNisidare, I hejejx (kAyaRkarxma) vihitavAdadedxMdu namage toVruvudilalx. 
\alnum{c} (\pArxparx) (muMde Aguvudanunx niriVkiSxsutAtx adakekx) pUvaRBAviyAgi. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{3} \eng{on view} noVDuvudakAkxgi, pariVkeSxgAgi, parishiVlanegAgi, avaloVkanakAkxgi -- parxdashiRsida. 
\num{4} \eng{private view} (citarx parxdashaRnada \vi) (senxVhitaru, vimashaRkaru, \mo) ApatxvagaRkekx mAtarx parxdashaRna; KAsagi parxdashaRna. 
\num{5} \eng{take a} \hyperref{kandict_d.pdf}{D}{dim(1) nuga}{$^1$dim} \eng{view of.} 
\num{6} \eng{take a} \hyperref{kandict_p.pdf}{P}{poor pagu(3)}{poor} \eng{view of.} 
\num{7} \eng{take the long-term view of} (yAvudeV \vi) dUrAloVcane mADu; BaviSayxvanunx ciMtisu. 
\num{8} \eng{to the view} bahiraMgavAgi; parxtayxkaSxvAgi; parxkaTavAgi; elalxrigU kANuvaMte. 
\numi{9} \eng{with a view to} 
\banum
\alnum{a} udedxVshadiMda yA niriVkeSxyiMda; guriyatatx oMdu hejejxyAgi. 
\alnum{b} (yAvudanenxV) paDeyuvudakAkxgi; (meVle) kaNiNxTuTx; paDeyuvudakokxVsakxra; paDeyuva saluvAgi: \eng{with a view to marriage} maduveya saluvAgi, daqSiTxyiMda. 
\eanum
\numie

\num{4} kasuvu, joVru, satatxvX, viVyaR, ceYtanayx, hurupu, Ojasusx -- uLaLx, iruva; deYhika shakitx yA caTuvaTike parxdashiRsuva (ciMtane, mAtu yA sheYliya \vi, \rUpa\ saha).

\expl{}

 bi viTaminf; deVhadalilx kelasa mADuva kelavu enfjeYmf kAyARcaraNege agatayxvAgiruva, niVrinalilx karaguva thayaminf, ribophelxvinf, piriDAkisxnf, sayanokobAlaminf muMtAda rAsAyanikavAgi parasapxra saMbaMdhisilalxdidadxrU halavomemx oMdeV AhAradalilx oTiTxge kANasiguva kAbaRnika saMyukatxgaLa guMpinalilx oMdu. \num{3}\eng{vitamin B6} = \hyperref{kandict_p.pdf}{P}{pyridoxine}{pyridoxine}. 
\num{4}\eng{vitamin B12} pArxNijanayx AhAravAda pitatxjanakAMga, miVnu matutx moTeTxgaLalilx kANbaruva, bi kAMpelxkfsx veYTaminf guMpige seVrida oMdu jiVvasatatxvX (idara korateyiMda parxbalavAda rakatxhiVnate uMTAgutatxde).

\bentry 
\word[voice(1)]{voice} 
\pron{vAyfsx} 
\gl{\nA}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} (dhavxninALadalilx huTiTx bAyalilx horaDuva, \kanmu\ manuSayxra) dhavxni; dani; shabadx; kaMTha; gaMTalu: \eng{I heard a voice} nanage oMdu dhavxni keVLisitu. \eng{he spoke in a low voice} avanu meludaniyalilx mAtanADida. \eng{I did not recognize her voice} nanage Akeya dhavxniya guruteV sigalilalx. \eng{the voice of the cuckoo} koVkila dhavxni; koVkilakaMTha. \eng{he has such a loud voice} avanige aSoTxMdu gaTiTxyAda dhavxni ide. 
\numi{2} 
\banum
\alnum{a} (mAtina \vi) ucAcxraNe. 
\alnum{b} (hADina \vi) kaMTha; shAriVra. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{3} gaMTalu; kaMTha; dhavxni(shakitx); shAriVra(bala): \eng{has lost her voice} avaLa shAriVra kugigxhoVgide. 
\num{4} mAtu; dani; nAlige; vAkukx; vANi; \kanmu\ ADida yA bareda padagaLu: \eng{he gave voice to his indignation in a pamphlet} avanu oMdu kiruhotatxgeyalilx tananx nAyxyavAda koVpavanunx padagaLalilx horageDahida, koVpakekx nAlige koTaTx. \eng{the dog gave voice to its joy} A nAyi tananx AnaMdavanunx kUginalilx sUcisitu. 
\numi{5} 
\banum
\alnum{a} mAtu; dhavxni; vayxkatxpaDisida aBipArxya. 
\alnum{b} aBipArxya koDuva hakukx: \eng{I have no voice in this matter} I viSayadalilx nanage aBipArxya koDuva hakikxlalx. 
\alnum{c} vANi; aBipArxya vayxkatxpaDisalu baLasuva vayxkitx yA sAdhana. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{6} (\dhavxni) GoVSavaNaR; dhavxnitaMtugaLa anuraNanadiMda yA kaMpanadiMda huTuTxva dhavxni. 
\num{7} (\vAyx) (kirxyApadada) kataRri, kamaRNi yA BAveV -- parxyoVga rUpa; kataRqvigU kirxyegU iruva saMbaMdhavanunx sUcisuva kirxyArUpagaLalilx oMdu. 
\numi{8} 
\banum

\alnum{b} (\saM) PUZyxgf eMba saMgiVta kaqtiya gAyanAMsha. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{9} (\sA\ \bava dalilx) deYvavANi; ashariVra, agoVcara -- dhavxni; adaqshayx Atamxvu mAgaRdashaRna mADalu nuDidudeMdu naMbalAda mAtu, dhavxni, shabadx. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent 
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum

\numi{2} \eng{in (good) voice} 
\banum
\alnum{a} (mAtanADuvudaralilx) oLeLxya ucAcxraNa shakitxyuLaLx. 
\alnum{b} (hADuvudaralilx) (utatxma) kaMThavuLaLx, shAriVravuLaLx. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{3} \eng{the voice of God} deYvavANi; deYva -- saMkalapx; korxVdha, shApa, \mo vugaLa aBivayxkitx. 
\num{4} \eng{with one voice} EkakaMThadiMda; EkABipArxyadiMda; okokxraliniMda; omamxtadiMda.

\bentry 
\word[voluntary(1)]{voluntary} 
\pron{vAlaMTari} 
\gl{\gu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} savx, savxyaM -- perxVrita; savxMta iSaTxdiMda, icePxyiMda -mADida yA mADuva yA mADabalalx; nibaRMdhitavAgi yA kaDADxyavAgi irada; savxsaMtoVSadiMda yA savxtaH mADida: \eng{voluntary contribution} savxsaMtoVSada kANike. 
\num{2} udedxVshapUvaRkavAda; icAPxpUvaRkavAda: \eng{voluntary waste} (hiDuvaLidAra yA bADigedAra mADida) udedxVshapUvaRkavAda nAsha, halAku. 
\num{3} veVtanarahita; saMbaLa ilalxda yA tegedukoLaLxda : \eng{voluntary work} veVtanarahita kelasa, udoyxVga. 
\num{4} (saMsethxya \vi) savxyaMperxVrita dAna, vaMtige, caMdA yA deVNigegaLiMda naDeyuva yA naDesuva. 
\num{5} (\birx) (shAleya \vi) savxyaMseVvA saMGavoMdu kaTiTxda Adare sathxLiVya shikaSxNa pArxdhikAravoMdu naDesuva, nivaRhisuva. 
\num{6} savxyaMseVveya; savxyaMperxVritavAgi mADida, utApxdisida, \mo. 
\num{7} (calane, mAMsaKaMDa yA aMgada \vi) saMkalapxpUvaRkavAda; icAPxniyaMtirxtavAda.

\bentry
\word[vote(1)]{vote} 
\pron{voVTf} 
\gl{\nA}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum

\numi{2} (\birx) 
\banum
\alnum{a} (sakARravu koVrida haNada \vi) (pAliRmeMTina) bahumatada anumoVdane. 
\alnum{b} bahumatABipArxya; bahumatadiMda vayxkatxvAda aBipArxya.

\numie
\num{3} voVTugaLa, matagaLa -- motatx; (oMdu pakaSx \mo vu yA oMdu pakaSx \mo vakekx koTaTx yA koDabahudAda oTuTx voVTugaLu): \eng{he will lose the Labour vote} avanu kAmiRka pakaSxda matagaLanunx kaLedukoLuLxvanu.

\num{5} voVTu ciVTi; voVTanunx gurutisalu baLasuva kAgada \mo vu. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent 
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} \eng{put to a} (\engit{or} \eng{the) vote} matakekx hAki niNaRyisu, niNaRyakekx oDuDx yA opipxsu. 
\num{2} \eng{take a vote on} (yAvudeV viSayada bagegx) mata tegeduko; (yAvudanenxV) matadAnada mUlaka niNaRyisu. 
\num{3} \eng{vote of censure} = \hyperlink{vote1 pagu5}{?pagu? \((5)\)}. 
\num{4} \eng{vote of confidence} vishAvxsa mata; ADaLita pakaSxvanunx adhikasaMKAyxtaru beMbalisuvareMdu toVrisuva bahumata. 
\hypertarget{vote1 pagu5}{} 
\num{5} \eng{vote of no confidence} avishAvxsa mata; ADaLita pakaSxvanunx adhika saMKAyxtaru beMbalisuvudilalxveMdu sUcisuva bahumata.

\word[vote(2)]{vote} 
\pron{voVTf} 
\gl{\sakirx}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\numi{1} voVTumADu; matahAku; bahumatadiMda 
\banum
\alnum{a} kAnUnu mADu. 
\alnum{b} TharAvanunx anumoVdisu. 
\alnum{c} haNa maMjUru mADu. 
\alnum{d} vayxkitxyanunx samiti \mo vugaLa sadasayxnanAnxgi cunAyisu yA samiti \mo vugaLa sadasayxtavxdiMda vajAmADu: \eng{was voted off} (\engit{or} \eng{voted out of) the committee} bahumata hAki avananunx samitiyiMda vajA mADalAyitu. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{2} (\AmA) savaRsamamxtiyiMda, savARnumatadiMda -- sAru, GoVSisu; sAmAnAyxBipArxyavAgi heVLu: \eng{the scheme was voted a failure} A yoVjane viPalavAyiteMdu (savaRsamamxtiyiMda) sAralAyitu. 
\num{3} (\AmA) tananx sUcaneyanunx horageDahu; salahe parxkaTapaDisu: \eng{I vote that we should go out on a picnic} nAvu oMdu vihArakAkxgi UriMdAce hoVgabeVkeMdu nAnu sUcisutetxVne, salahe mADutetxVne. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent 
\gl{\akirx}
\expl{}
\bmng
mata -- hAku, calAyisu; voVTu mADu. 
\emng

\noindent 
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\hypertarget{vote2 pagu1}{} 
\bnum
\num{1} \eng{vote down} (sUcane \mo vanunx bahumatadiMda) taLiLxhAku; nirAkarisu; soVlisu; viPalagoLisu. 
\num{2} \eng{vote in} voVTugaLa mUlaka -- AyekxmADu, cunAyisu. 
\numi{3} \eng{vote out} 
\banum
\alnum{a} (vayxkitxyanunx samiti \mo vugaLa) sadasayxtavxdiMda vajAmADu, horadUDu. 
\alnum{b} = \hyperlink{vote2 pagu1}{?pagu? \((1)\)}. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{4} \eng{vote with one's feet} (\AmA) (obabxnu) tananx hAjarAtiyiMda yA geYruhAjariyiMda tananx aBipArxyavanunx sUcisu. 
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\bentry

\pron{vw}
\gl{\nA}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\numi{1} (BagavaMtanige, yAvudeV deVvatege, saMtanige, saMtaLige) 
\banum
\alnum{a} (parxmANa mADikoTaTx) vacana; shapatha; parxtijecnx; ANe; BASe. 
\alnum{b} (kaTiTxkoMDa) harake; (kaTiTxTaTx) muDupu. 
\alnum{c} keYgoMDa varxta, noVMpi. 
\hypertarget{vow(1)2}{} 
\eanum
\numie
\num{2} jAcnxnasAnxnada -- parxtijecnxgaLu, parxmANagaLu; jAcnxnasAnxnada kAladalilx A saMsAkxra paDedavanAgali, Atana dhamiVRya pitaneV \mo\ baMdhugaLAgali, keYgoLuLxva parxtijecnx. 
\hypertarget{vow(1)3}{} 
\num{3} (\bava dalilx) parxNayigaLa yA satipatiyara parasapxra niSAThxparxtijecnxgaLu; avaru obabxrigobabxru parapuruSa, parasitxrXVyaranunx kAmisade, parasapxra dorxVha esagade, iruveveMdu mADuva parxmANagaLu. 
\hypertarget{vow(1)4}{} 
\num{4} (\bava dalilx) (saMnAyxsi yA saMnAyxsiniyu veYrAgayx, barxhamxcayaR yA sAdhivxVtavx matutx saMyamagaLige AjiVva badadhxrAgiruvudAgi diVkASxkAladalilx parxmANa mADuva) saMnAyxsa parxtijecnxgaLu yA diVkASxparxtijecnxgaLu. 
\enum
